<td style=" text-align: center;margin:auto; vertical-align:top"><ix:nonNumeric name="dei:TradingSymbol" contextRef="duration_2024-07-24_to_2024-07-24_us-gaap-StatementClassOfStockAxis_tmus-M3.550SeniorNotesDue2029Member" id="ixv-408">TMUS29</ix:nonNumeric></td>

<td style="vertical-align:bottom">&#160;</td>
<td style=" text-align: center;margin:auto; vertical-align:top"><ix:nonNumeric name="dei:TradingSymbol" contextRef="duration_2024-07-24_to_2024-07-24_us-gaap-StatementClassOfStockAxis_tmus-M3.700SeniorNotesDue2032Member" id="ixv-411">TMUS32</ix:nonNumeric></td>
<td style="vertical-align:bottom">&#160;</td>
<td style=" text-align: center;margin:auto; vertical-align:top"><ix:nonNumeric name="dei:SecurityExchangeName" contextRef="duration_2024-07-24_to_2024-07-24_us-gaap-StatementClassOfStockAxis_tmus-M3.700SeniorNotesDue2032Member" format="ixt-sec:exchnameen" id="ixv-412">The NASDAQ Stock Market LLC</ix:nonNumeric></td></tr>

<td style="vertical-align:bottom">&#160;</td>
<td style=" text-align: center;margin:auto; vertical-align:top"><ix:nonNumeric name="dei:TradingSymbol" contextRef="duration_2024-07-24_to_2024-07-24_us-gaap-StatementClassOfStockAxis_tmus-M3.850SeniorNotesDue2036Member" id="ixv-414">TMUS36</ix:nonNumeric></td>
<td style="vertical-align:bottom">&#160;</td>
<td style=" text-align: center;margin:auto; vertical-align:top"><ix:nonNumeric name="dei:SecurityExchangeName" contextRef="duration_2024-07-24_to_2024-07-24_us-gaap-StatementClassOfStockAxis_tmus-M3.850SeniorNotesDue2036Member" format="ixt-sec:exchnameen" id="ixv-415">The NASDAQ Stock Market LLC</ix:nonNumeric></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Indicate by check mark whether the registrant is an emerging growth company as defined in Rule 405 of the Securities Act of 1933 (&#167;230.405 of this chapter) or Rule <span style="white-space:nowrap">12b-2</span> of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 <span style="white-space:nowrap">(&#167;240.12b-2</span> of this chapter).</p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Emerging growth company&#8194;<ix:nonNumeric name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany" contextRef="duration_2024-07-24_to_2024-07-24" format="ixt-sec:boolballotbox" id="ixv-416">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If an emerging growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section&#160;13(a) of the Exchange Act.&#8194;&#9744;</p> <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p> <p style="line-height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&#160;</p> <p style="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&#160;</p></div></div>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%;clear:both"/>

<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;7.01 &#8212; Regulation FD Disclosure. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On July&#160;24, 2024, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> US, Inc. (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline"><span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span></span>&#8221;) and KKR&#160;&amp; Co. Inc. (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">KKR</span>&#8221;) issued a joint press release announcing that they have entered into a definitive agreement to establish a joint venture (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">JV</span>&#8221;) to acquire Metronet Holdings, LLC and certain of its affiliates (collectively, &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Metronet</span>&#8221;), including Metronet&#8217;s broadband infrastructure, residential fiber business operations and existing customers. As part of the transaction, the JV will also acquire Oak Hill Capital&#8217;s existing stake. Oak Hill Capital will <span style="white-space:nowrap">re-invest</span> to retain a minority position and founder John Cinelli will also retain a minority position in the business following close of the transaction. In connection with the completion of the transaction, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and the JV will enter into an Asset Purchase Agreement, pursuant to which, among other things, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> will acquire Metronet&#8217;s residential fiber retail operations and customers, and a <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span style="white-space:nowrap"><span style="white-space:nowrap">Fiber-to-the-Premises</span></span></span> Master Framework Agreement, pursuant to which, among other things, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> will purchase wholesale fiber services from Metronet and become the exclusive seller of Metronet&#8217;s residential fiber services. <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> will market and sell such services under the <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> brand. A copy of the joint press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 hereto and is incorporated by reference herein. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The transaction is expected to close in 2025, subject to customary closing conditions and regulatory approvals. <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> expects to invest approximately $4.9&#160;billion to acquire a 50% equity stake in the JV at the closing and, pursuant to the Asset Purchase Agreement, 100% of Metronet&#8217;s residential fiber retail operations and customers, as well as funding of the JV. The JV is expected to be self-funding on a <span style="white-space:nowrap">go-forward</span> basis, and <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> does not anticipate contributing any additional future capital to the JV following the closing to support the current business plan to reach an aggregate of approximately 6.5&#160;million homes passed by the end of 2030. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The operating agreement of the JV will provide that from the fourth to the seventh anniversary of the closing, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> will have an option to purchase a number of newly issued units of the JV to reach 50.01% ownership in the JV, subject to the terms and conditions contained therein. In addition, from the fifth (or in certain circumstances the fourth) to the seventh anniversary of the closing, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> will have an option to purchase KKR&#8217;s interest in the JV at fair market value at the time of exercising such option, subject to certain specified guaranteed minimum and maximum internal rates of return and other terms and conditions (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Completion Call</span>&#8221;). </p>
</div></div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%;clear:both"/>

<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Following the closing, the board of directors of the JV will consist of two directors appointed by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> two directors appointed by KKR and one independent director. If <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> elects to exercise the call option to reach 50.01% ownership in the JV, the board of directors of the JV will consist of three directors appointed by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and two directors appointed by KKR. Certain actions by the JV will require the approval of at least one director appointed by KKR and at least one director appointed by <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and certain actions require the consent of each of KKR and <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</span> </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The operating agreement of the JV will provide that the JV will be the only vehicle through which <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and certain affiliates of KKR will build, own or operate fixed wireline broadband services network to homes in certain geographic locations in the United States, subject to certain exceptions for mergers and acquisitions and other matters. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Following the closing of the transaction, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> expects to report the customers purchased from Metronet as <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> customers, with the associated residential fiber customer operating revenues reflected in Service Revenues and wholesale costs paid to the JV for network access reflected in Cost of Services. <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> interests in the JV will be reflected in <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> Consolidated Balance Sheet as an investment within Other Assets and <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> share of the net income of the JV will be included in Consolidated Statement of Comprehensive Income under the equity method of accounting. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> expects that its current business plan, after assuming a successful completion of this proposed transaction and previously announced pending transactions, continues to support a stockholder remuneration plan of up to $60&#160;billion by <span style="white-space:nowrap">mid-2026.</span> </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This information, including Exhibit 99.1, is being furnished to the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">SEC</span>&#8221;) and shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Exchange Act</span>&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section. This information shall not be incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing. This Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> will not be deemed an admission as to the materiality of any of the information contained in this Item 7.01, including Exhibit 99.1. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Cautionary Statement Regarding Forward-Looking Statements </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This communication contains certain forward-looking statements concerning <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and the proposed transaction with KKR to acquire Metronet. There are several factors which could cause actual plans and results to differ materially from those expressed or implied in forward-looking statements. negative effects of the pendency or consummation of the proposed transaction on the market price of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> common stock and on <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> operating results; <HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE" STYLE="line-height:Normal">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and KKR Announce Joint </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Venture to Acquire Metronet and Offer </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Leading Fiber Solution to More U.S. Consumers </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> will expand its broadband portfolio and&nbsp;offer more</I> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>consumers a differentiated&nbsp;experience,&nbsp;selling&nbsp;fiber internet services</I> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>provided by the JV&nbsp;using Metronet&#146;s fiber network deployment and management expertise</I> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>BELLEVUE, Wash., NEW YORK, NY, and EVANSVILLE, Ind. &#151; July, 24, 2024 &#151;</B> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> (NASDAQ: TMUS),
America&#146;s 5G leader and fastest-growing fixed wireless broadband provider, today announced it has entered into a definitive agreement to establish a joint venture (JV) with leading global investment firm KKR (NYSE: KKR) that will acquire
Metronet, including its broadband infrastructure, rapidly growing residential fiber business operations and existing customers. As part of the transaction, the JV will also acquire Oak Hill Capital&#146;s existing stake. Oak Hill Capital will <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">re-invest</FONT> to retain a minority position and founder John Cinelli will also retain a minority position once the deal closes. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Metronet is uniquely positioned as the fastest-growing pure play fiber company in the U.S. and an experienced independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">fiber-to-the-home</FONT></FONT></FONT> (FTTH) operator. The company currently reaches more than 2&nbsp;million homes and businesses across 17 states with fiber solutions built on a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">state-of-the</FONT></FONT> art broadband platform. Following the transaction&#146;s close, Metronet will become a wholesale services provider for its retail customers and 100% of its
residential fiber retail operations and customers will transition to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> will have full responsibility for residential customer acquisition and support,
leveraging its differentiated retail, marketing, brand and service model, and will utilize Metronet&#146;s deep digital and fiber infrastructure expertise to expand to more households with fiber broadband services. Metronet will focus on build
plans, network engineering and design, network deployment, and customer installation. Following the transaction close, Metronet is expected to be self-funding on a go forward basis and it is expected to reach 6.5&nbsp;million homes passed by the end
of 2030. To support this business plan <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> does not expect to make any additional capital contributions to the JV. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;This is a unique opportunity and a smart, capital-efficient deal that enables <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> to profitably build on
our success in broadband and provide fast, affordable and reliable connectivity options to millions more customers nationwide as a complement to our wireless growth strategy,&#148; said Mike Sievert, CEO of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> &#147;Metronet is the perfect partner for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> as a leader in fiber solutions with an incredibly fast build pace, and a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-notch</FONT> management team. Together with KKR&#146;s strong heritage of corporate partnership and global fiber franchise, we will further expand the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier&#146;s</FONT>
fiber footprint and deliver real value and choice to customers while addressing a growing demand for fast and reliable broadband.&#148; </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;As a leading investor in fiber broadband, KKR has a strong track record of building fiber networks in
multiple countries around the world. Since our initial investment in Metronet in 2021, the company has grown rapidly, including constructing new fiber infrastructure and adding subscribers in attractive, underserved markets,&#148; said Waldemar
Szlezak, Partner, and Global Head of Digital Infrastructure at KKR. &#147;Our new joint venture with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> will be transformational for the future of the Metronet business. We look forward to benefitting
from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> industry-leading customer experience to support the company in reaching its full potential.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The JV will be complementary to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> already existing 5G Home Internet offering, a fixed wireless solution
currently being used in more than 5&nbsp;million households and businesses nationwide using fallow network capacity over the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier&#146;s</FONT> 5G network, and the company&#146;s previously announced fiber
partnerships. This expanded portfolio of offerings will help meet continually increasing consumer demand for higher speed and reliable broadband products. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We could not be prouder to expand our strategic partnership with KKR and form a new one with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> &#151; two
global leaders in 5G wireless connectivity and digital infrastructure,&#148; said Metronet CEO Dave Heimbach. &#147;Metronet&#146;s 100% fiber network delivers symmetrical multi-gigabit internet service directly to homes and businesses, perfectly
complementing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> industry-leading 5G mobile and fixed-wireless offerings to meet consumer demand for seamless, ubiquitous connectivity. With this new partnership, Metronet will expand its fiber
network faster and farther, reaching millions more households by the end of the decade.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">KKR is making the investment in Metronet through its global
infrastructure strategy. The firm first established its global infrastructure strategy in 2008 and has since been one of the most active infrastructure investors around the world, currently managing over $61&nbsp;billion in infrastructure assets.
KKR has significant experience investing in the growth of leading FTTH providers globally with over 25&nbsp;million homes passed and building more than four million annually. This includes the creation of independent open access wholesale fiber
optic network companies in Chile, Colombia, Peru and in the Netherlands and investments in Hyperoptic in the U.K., Telenor Fiber in Norway and Deutsche Glasfaser in Germany. Most recently, KKR announced the closing of its acquisition of Telecom
Italia Netco, which owns and operates the entire national copper and fiber fixed line network in Italy. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The transaction is expected to close in 2025,
subject to customary closing conditions and regulatory approvals. At closing, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> is expected to invest approximately $4.9&nbsp;billion to acquire a 50% equity stake in the JV and 100% of Metronet&#146;s
residential fiber retail operations and customers, as well as funding of the JV. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Cautionary Statement Regarding Forward-Looking Statements</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This communication contains certain forward-looking statements concerning <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and the proposed transaction with
KKR to acquire Metronet&#146;s broadband infrastructure. All statements other than statements of fact, including information concerning future results, are forward-looking statements. These forward-looking statements are generally identified by the
words &#147;plan,&#148; &#147;anticipate,&#148; &#147;believe,&#148; &#147;estimate,&#148; &#147;expect,&#148; &#147;intend,&#148; &#147;may,&#148; &#147;could&#148; or similar expressions. Such forward-looking statements include, but are not

intentions, expectations regarding the JV being self-funding and future contributions (or lack thereof), the expected number of homes passed by the JV in the future and the expected timing of completion of the proposed transaction. There are several
factors which could cause actual plans and results to differ materially from those expressed or implied in forward-looking statements. Such factors include, but are not limited to, the failure to satisfy any of the conditions to the proposed
transaction on a timely basis or at all; the occurrence of events that may give rise to a right of one or both </P>
</DIV></Center>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc. (NASDAQ: TMUS) is America&#146;s supercharged <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier,</FONT> delivering an advanced 4G LTE and transformative nationwide 5G network that will offer reliable
connectivity for all. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> customers benefit from its unmatched combination of value and quality, unwavering obsession with offering them the best possible service experience and undisputable drive
for disruption that creates competition and innovation in wireless and beyond. Based in Bellevue, Wash., <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> provides services through its subsidiaries and operates its flagship brands, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Metro by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Mint Mobile. For more information please visit: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">https://www.t-mobile.com</FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About KKR </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">KKR is a leading global investment firm that
offers alternative asset management as well as capital markets and insurance solutions. KKR aims to generate attractive investment returns by following a patient and disciplined investment approach, employing world-class people, and supporting
growth in its portfolio companies and communities. KKR sponsors investment funds that invest in private equity, credit and real assets and has strategic partners that manage hedge funds. KKR&#146;s insurance subsidiaries offer retirement, life and
reinsurance products under the management of Global Atlantic Financial Group. References to KKR&#146;s investments may include the activities of its sponsored funds and insurance subsidiaries. For additional information about KKR&nbsp;&amp; Co. Inc.
(NYSE: KKR), please visit KKRs website at www.kkr.com. For additional information about Global Atlantic Financial Group, please visit Global Atlantic Group&#146;s website at www.globalatlantic.com. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Metronet </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Metronet is <I>PCMag</I>&#146;s
&#147;Fastest Major ISP&#148; for 2023 and 2024, providing multi-gigabit internet service to homes and businesses in cities like Colorado Springs, Des Moines, Indianapolis, Lexington, Norfolk, Tallahassee and more than 300 other communities across
17 states. Expanding its fiber-optic network in more than 90 communities at any one time, Metronet has become the country&#146;s largest and fastest growing privately owned <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">fiber-to-the-home</FONT></FONT></FONT> company. More information on the Evansville, Ind.-based company can be found at metronet.com. </P>
